[ 
  =, 
  'mc_2__|-'( 
     [ [  [ _A, x|...], -->, _R], 
       _T1], 
     [ [  [ _C, x|...], -->, _R], 
       _T2], 
     A), 
  [ [ assign, 
      B, 
       [ _C, -->|...]], 
    [ assign, 
      C, 
      [ call('Truth_Abduction'), '$VAR'('_T1'), '$VAR'('_T2')]], 
    [ assign, '$VAR'(0), list( [ '$VAR'(...)|...])]]].

'mc_2__|-'([[[_A, x, _B], -->, _R], _T1], [[[_C, x, _B], -->, _R], _T2], A) :-
    B=[_C, -->, _A],

    A=[B, C].

transpiler_clause_store('|-', 3, 12, ['Any', 'Any'], 'AnyRet', [x(doeval, eager), x(doeval, eager)], x(doeval, eager), ['|-', [[_R, -->, [_A, x, _B]], _T1], [[_R, -->, [_C, x, _B]], _T2]], [[_C, -->, _A], ['Truth_Induction', _T1, _T2]]).

[ 
  =, 
  'mc_2__|-'( 
     [ [ _R, 
         -->, 
          [ _A, x|...]], 
       _T1], 
     [ [ _R, 
         -->, 
          [ _C, x|...]], 
       _T2], 
     A), 
  [ [ assign, 
      B, 
       [ _C, -->|...]], 
    [ assign, 
      C, 
      [ call('Truth_Induction'), '$VAR'('_T1'), '$VAR'('_T2')]], 
    [ assign, '$VAR'(0), list( [ '$VAR'(...)|...])]]].

'mc_2__|-'([[_R, -->, [_A, x, _B]], _T1], [[_R, -->, [_C, x, _B]], _T2], A) :-
    B=[_C, -->, _A],
    mc_2__Truth_Induction(_T1, _T2, C),
    A=[B, C].

'mc_2__|-'([[_R, -->, [_A, x, _B]], _T1], [[_R, -->, [_C, x, _B]], _T2], A) :-
    B=[_C, -->, _A],
